<dl>
<dt>Notes</dt>
<dd><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_.E2.98.AF"><b><a href="#ref_.E2.98.AF">^DVI compatible</a></b></span> HDMI signal can be converted to DVI by passive adapter.</dd>
<dd><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_.E2.99.BF"><b><a href="#ref_.E2.99.BF">^DVI incompatible</a></b></span> HDMI signal not convertible to DVI by passive adapter. Watch out for HDMI screens that require DVI signalling.</dd>
</dl>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Operating_system">Operating system</span></h2>
<table class="wikitable sortable" border="1" style="font-size: 85%; text-align:center;">
<tr>
<th scope="col">Name</th>
<th scope="col" style="width: 35em">Linux</th>
<th scope="col">Android</th>
<th scope="col">BSD</th>
<th scope="col">Windows</th>
<th scope="col">Other</th>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Arduino Uno</td>

<dl>
<dt>Notes</dt>
<dd><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_imx6"><b><a href="#ref_imx6">^i.MX6</a></b></span>&#160;: mainline Linux has basic support (<a href="/wiki/Device_tree" title="Device tree">device trees</a>) for most i.MX6 boards<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67"><span>[</span>67<span>]</span></a></sup> (including Nitrogen6x, Wandboard, RIoTboard), but board vendors may still recommend forked kernels for full functionality. Vivante GPU drivers are provided as userspace library BLOBs;<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68"><span>[</span>68<span>]</span></a></sup> a future open-source alternative might be <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/laanwj/etna_viv">etnaviv</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-etnaviv-coming_69-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-etnaviv-coming-69"><span>[</span>69<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
